$(top_level_links).next('ul').attr({ 'aria-hidden': 'true', 'role': 'menu' }).find('a').attr('tabIndex', -1);\n\n        // Adding aria-haspopup for appropriate items\n        $(top_level_links).each(function () {\n            if ($(this).next('ul').length > 0)\n                $(this).parent('li').attr('aria-haspopup', 'true');\n        });\n\n        $(top_level_links).focus(function () {\n            //hide open menus\n            hideChannelMenu();\n\n            if ($(this).parent('li').find('ul').length > 0) {\n                $(this).parent('li').addClass(settings.menuHoverClass).find('ul').css('display', 'block');\n            }\n        });\n\n        // Bind arrow keys for navigation\n        $(top_level_links).keydown(function (e) {\n            if (e.keyCode == 37) { //key left\n                e.preventDefault();\n\n                // This is the first item\n                if ($(this).parent('li').prev('li').length == 0) {\n                    $(this).parents('ul').find('> li').last().find('a').first().focus();\n                } else {\n                    $(this).parent('li').prev('li').find('a').first().focus();\n                }\n            } else if (e.keyCode == 38) { //key up\n                e.preventDefault();\n\n                if ($(this).parent('li').find('ul').length > 0) {\n                    $(this).parent('li').addClass(settings.menuHoverClass).find('ul').css('display', 'block').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').find('a').attr('tabIndex', 0).last().focus();\n                }\n            } else if (e.keyCode == 39) { //key right\n                e.preventDefault();\n\n                // This is the last item\n                if ($(this).parent('li').next('li').length == 0) {\n                    $(this).parents('ul').find('> li').first().find('a').first().focus();\n                } else {\n                    $(this).parent('li').next('li').find('a').first().focus();\n                }\n            } else if (e.keyCode == 40) { //key down\n                e.preventDefault();\n\n                if ($(this).parent('li').find('ul').length > 0) {\n                    $(this).parent('li')\n                         .addClass(settings.menuHoverClass)\n                         .find('ul').css('display', 'block')\n                         .attr('aria-hidden', 'false')\n                         .find('a').attr('tabIndex', 0)\n                         .first().focus();\n                }\n            } else if (e.keyCode == 13 || e.keyCode == 32) { //enter key\n                // If submenu is hidden, open it\n                e.preventDefault();\n\n                $(this).parent('li').find('ul[aria-hidden=true]').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').addClass(settings.menuHoverClass).find('a').attr('tabIndex', 0).first().focus();\n            } else if (e.keyCode == 27) { //escape key\n                e.preventDefault();\n                hideChannelMenu();\n            } else {\n                $(this).parent('li').find('ul[aria-hidden=false] a').each(function () {\n                    if ($(this).text().substring(0, 1).toLowerCase() == keyCodeMap[e.keyCode]) {\n                        $(this).focus();\n                        return false;\n                    }\n                });\n            }\n        });\n\n        var links = $(top_level_links).parent('li').find('ul').find('a');\n\n        $(links).keydown(function (e) {\n            if (e.keyCode == 38) {\n                e.preventDefault();\n\n                // This is the first item\n                if ($(this).parent('li').prev('li').length == 0) {\n                    $(this).parents('ul').parents('li').find('a').first().focus();\n                } else {\n                    $(this).parent('li').prev('li').find('a').first().focus();\n                }\n            } else if (e.keyCode == 40) {\n                e.preventDefault();\n\n                if ($(this).parent('li').next('li').length == 0) {\n                    $(this).parents('ul').parents('li').find('a').first().focus();\n                } else {\n                    $(this).parent('li').next('li').find('a').first().focus();\n                }\n            } else if (e.keyCode == 27 || e.keyCode == 37) {\n                e.preventDefault();\n\n                $(this).parents('ul').first().prev('a').focus().parents('ul').first().find('.' + settings.menuHoverClass).attr('aria-hidden', 'true').removeClass(settings.menuHoverClass).find('a').attr('tabIndex', -1);\n            } else if (e.keyCode == 32) {\n                e.preventDefault();\n                window.location = $(this).attr('href');\n            } else {\n                var found = false;\n\n                $(this).parent('li').nextAll('li').find('a').each(function () {\n                    if ($(this).text().substring(0, 1).toLowerCase() == keyCodeMap[e.keyCode]) {\n                        $(this).focus();\n                        found = true;\n                        return false;\n                    }\n                });\n\n                if (!found) {\n                    $(this).parent('li').prevAll('li').find('a').each(function () {\n                        if ($(this).text().substring(0, 1).toLowerCase() == keyCodeMap[e.keyCode]) {\n                            $(this).focus();\n                            return false;\n                        }\n                    });\n                }\n            }\n        });\n\n        function hideChannelMenu() {\n            $('li.sw-channel-item.' + settings.menuHoverClass).attr('aria-hidden', 'true').removeClass(settings.menuHoverClass).find('ul').css('display', 'none').find('a').attr('tabIndex', -1);\n        }\n\n        // Hide menu if click or focus occurs outside of navigation\n        $('[id=\"channel-navigation\"]').find('a').last().keydown(function (e) {\n            if (e.keyCode == 9) {\n                // If the user tabs out of the navigation hide all menus\n                hideChannelMenu();\n            }\n        });\n\n        $('[id=\"channel-navigation\"]').find('a').first().keydown(function (e) {\n            if (e.keyCode == 9) {\n                // hide open MyStart Bar menus\n                hideMyStartBarMenu();\n            }\n        });\n\n        /*$(document).click(function() {\n            hideChannelMenu();\n        });*/\n\n        $('[id=\"channel-navigation\"]').click(function (e) {\n            e.stopPropagation();\n        });\n    });\n    </script>\n\n    <!-- Page -->\n    \n    <style type=\"text/css\">/* MedaiBegin Standard *//*\nfont-family: 'Merriweather Sans', } else if (e.keyCode == 40) {\n                e.preventDefault();\n\n                if ($(this).parent('li').next('li').length == 0) {\n                    $(this).parents('ul').parents('li').find('a').first().focus();\n                } else {\n                    $(this).parent('li').next('li').find('a').first().focus();\n                }\n            } else if (e.keyCode == 27 || e.keyCode == 37) {\n                e.preventDefault();\n\n                $(this).parents('ul').first().prev('a').focus().parents('ul').first().find('.' + settings.menuHoverClass).attr('aria-hidden', 'true').removeClass(settings.menuHoverClass).find('a').attr('tabIndex', -1);\n            } else if (e.keyCode == 32) {\n                e.preventDefault();\n                window.location = $(this).attr('href');\n            } else {\n                var found = false;\n\n                $(this).parent('li').nextAll('li').find('a').each(function () {\n                    if ($(this).text().substring(0, 1).toLowerCase() == keyCodeMap[e.keyCode]) {\n                        $(this).focus();\n                        found = true;\n                        return false;\n                    }\n                });\n\n                if (!found) {\n                    $(this).parent('li').prevAll('li').find('a').each(function () {\n                        if ($(this).text().substring(0, 1).toLowerCase() == keyCodeMap[e.keyCode]) {\n                            $(this).focus();\n                            return false;\n                        }\n                    });\n                }\n            }\n        });\n\n        function hideChannelMenu() {\n            $('li.sw-channel-item.' + settings.menuHoverClass).attr('aria-hidden', 'true').removeClass(settings.menuHoverClass).find('ul').css('display', 'none').find('a').attr('tabIndex', -1);\n        }\n\n        // Hide menu if click or focus occurs outside of navigation\n        $('[id=\"channel-navigation\"]').find('a').last().keydown(function (e) {\n            if (e.keyCode == 9) {\n                // If the user tabs out of the navigation hide all menus\n                hideChannelMenu();\n            }\n        });\n\n clickable on second click. first click simply opens the menu.\n        $('#channel-navigation > .sw-channel-item > a').on({\n            'touchstart': function (e) {\n                \n                // see if has menu\n                if ($(this).siblings('ul.sw-channel-dropdown').length > 0) {\n                    var button = $(this);\n\n                    // add href as property if not already set\n                    // then remove href attribute\n                    if (!button.prop('linkHref')) {\n                        button.prop('linkHref', button.attr('href'));\n                        button.removeAttr('href');\n                    }\n\n                    // check to see if menu is already open\n                    if
